***смеяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смеяться.html>смея́ться</a> (674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-смея́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-smejátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*smьjati</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смеяться.html>смея́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smejátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:засмеяться.html>засмея́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посмеяться.html>посмея́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to laugh</li>
<li>to laugh at (<a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>ке́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смеяться.html>смеёшься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>на́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мно́й</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Počemú ty <b>smejóšʹsja</b> nád mnój?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Why are you laughing at me?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to mock, to deride</li></ol>

***смирить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смирить.html>смири́ть</a> (30548)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съмѣрити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭměriti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mitigate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. After regular assimilation <i>ѣ</i>…<i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и́</a></i> gt; <i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i>…<i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и́</a></i> reanalysed as a derivative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирить.html>мири́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смирить.html>смири́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smirítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смирять.html>смиря́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to humble, to tame</li>
<li>to suppress, to restrain (an emotion)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смириться.html>смири́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smirítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усмирить.html>усмири́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">usmirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смиренный.html>смире́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smirénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смирный.html>сми́рный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smírnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:инструктор.html>Инстру́ктор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a>: ― <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>Е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скомандовать.html>скома́ндую</a> «<span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:смирно.html>сми́рно</a></span>», <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a> ― <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дышать.html>дыши́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:замереть.html>замри́</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>Забу́дь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отца́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>мать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зову́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слушать.html>слу́шай</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> дальше <a href = vnd.unilang:последовать.html>последует</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смирявшийся.html>смиря́вшийся</a> (27944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смоделировать.html>смодели́ровать</a> (25211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моделировать.html>модели́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">modɛlírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смоделировать.html>смодели́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smodɛlírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моделировать.html>модели́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to model, to design, to fashion, to shape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to simulate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">art</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to model, to sculpture</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смокинг.html>смо́кинг</a> (18354)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">smoking</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">smoking jacket</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***смола.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смола́</a> (5532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смола́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smola</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*smola</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смола́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smolá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смолы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смо́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смо́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>resin, pitch, tar, coal tar (viscous liquid of plant origin)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">смоль</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smolʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***смолкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смолкать.html>смолка́ть</a> (17094)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смолкнуть.html>смо́лкнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smólknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смолкать.html>смолка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smolkátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смолкнуть.html>смо́лкнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(sound, noise)</i> to cease, to stop</li>
<li>to grow silent, to fall into silence, to fall silent</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***смолкнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смолкнуть.html>смо́лкнуть</a> (6471)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мо́лкнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mólknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смолкнуть.html>смо́лкнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smólknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смолкать.html>смолка́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(sound, noise)</i> to cease, to stop</li>
<li>to grow silent, to fall into silence, to fall silent</li></ol>

***смольный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смольный.html>смо́льный</a> (10600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смола́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smolá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смольный.html>смо́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smólʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resin, tar</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resinous, tarry</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смоляной.html>смоляно́й</a> (17990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смола́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smolá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-яно́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-janój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смоляной.html>смоляно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smoljanój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tar, pitch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смоляной.html>смоляна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smoljanája</b> jáma</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>tar</b> pit</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tarry <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">resembling tar</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>tarred <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">covered with tar</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jet-black, pitch-black, glossy black
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смоляной.html>смоляны́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smoljanýje</b> vólosy</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>jet-black</b> hair</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">covered with tar</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">смолёный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smoljónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">просмолённый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prosmoljónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
